<h2>IAUC Text-Item Titles:  IAUCs 1-8000</h2>
<p><hr><p>
     Note that these titles have not all been fully checked, but
they should be in reasonable shape.  This should be thus considered
as a temporary list, but it is being made available for the benefit
of researchers.  The process of getting all IAUCs online here, back
to IAUC 1, is underway and will hopefully be complete by
2008.  In the list below, "C*" means "corrigendum to IAUC".
The 4-digit IAU Circular number is given in columns 3-6; the "4"
in column 1 is an internal indexing code (and appears on all
records below).  [As this is a plain-ASCII list, the diacritical
marks have been omitted.]
<p><hr><p>
<pre>
